msg:I decided to stay at JEN late that day. I had read a lot of reviews on Xiaohongshu before, so I was looking forward to it and curious. I would like to share some of my feelings:

Disadvantages:

1. The front desk service was cold:

I didn't know this hotel was from Shangri-La before, but it is a luxury hotel. I felt very cold and didn't talk much when I checked in.

2. The lobby was chaotic and there were safety risks:
It was basically after 10 o'clock in the evening when I checked in. In addition to the lively a**osphere of the fresh beer bar, there were many children playing and fighting, and even three or five of them were lying at my feet. Even if the parents didn't care, there was no work during this period. The staff reminded or stopped them, and these children who were playing and running around were always running between the gate and the reception area. The distance between them was originally very short and the space was small. If the children bumped into other guests, it would easily cause disputes between parents and other customers, and the safety was also poor.

3. The bathroom space was cramped:
It was labeled as a five-star luxury hotel, but the bathroom was small and there was almost no place to put things on the washbasin, similar to a fast hotel. I stayed alone and there was only a little space for a cosmetic bag. After washing, the water would definitely splash the cosmetic bag and the surrounding area. Because I arrived late, I didn‚Äôt feel the night bed Service, if there is a night bed, the toiletries in this area cannot be laid out for you. In short, for two people, the washbasin is not enough. Of course, it may also be that my room is not big enough.

4. Poor attitude of the staff on the 3rd floor:
I made an appoin**ent with a friend to meet at the mall. When I went to the 3rd floor, I walked directly into the hotel meeting area because I didn‚Äôt know the direction. Suddenly, a staff member stopped me and asked me where I was going. After I said I was going to the mall, I was directly told, "This is the hotel, you can't enter here, go over there to the mall." The tough attitude made me very embarrassed.

5. Suggestions for content details and text errors :
Maybe due to the nature of my work, I saw the content on the bathroom sign and suggested some changes. Many details of your hotel reflect high CSR and environmental sustainable development actions and concepts, but the text says "corporate social responsibility" as "social corporate responsibility". As a profitable international hotel management company, you are a profit-making legal entity, not a "social enterprise" legally recognized by the state. Such a statement is not only easy to cause ambiguity, but also shows that the hotel team is not rigorous in the details of content output. I suggest some changes. Of course, it is OK not to change it. It depends on how much you value this matter.

Advantages:
1. Excellent geographical environment:
If you want to be in the China World Mall and nearby areas, the location is very good

2. The view is great
For guests who like the view of the East Third Ring Road, the hotel view will satisfy your viewing and photography needs

3. Excellent concierge service
From getting off the car, helping with luggage, sending upstairs, to room introduction, subsequent express parcels, luggage storage, I must praise the concierge. Several men are the best place for me to experience this hotel

The room is clean and tidy, but relatively small. For hotels in the China World Mall area, it is suitable for young people. The decoration and service are more inclined to high-end boutique hotels. If you want to talk about cost-effectiveness, the value point lies in the geographical location and landscape, as well as the trendy design of the hotel. In terms of hardware, service, and modernization, it is still far from a real luxury hotel.

Lobby:
To be honest, it's a bit crude and relatively small in size, but after all, it is directly built in the China World Trade Center, and the first three floors can directly lead to the interior of the China World Trade Center, which is completely understandable to me.

Serve:
The attitude of the waiter was also very good during the ci. I expressed my need to see "big underpants". The manager Liang who was on duty that day changed my room very readily. Many thanks to him!

Room:
The floor-to-ceiling windows have a great view! If you look up, you will see the China Zun, if you look to the left, you will see the CCTV building, and if you look to the right, you will see the continuous traffic in Beijing. The moment you open the door at night is really amazing. In terms of bedding, anyway, I didn't notice the difference between sleeping and lux. The comfort is perfect and I have a good rest. However, there is one point about the bathroom. They do not have a fixed ceiling shower in the shower room of the basic room. I was quite disappointed at first. After all, I always think that this thing is a standard configuration. But after experiencing their ordinary shower, my troubles disappeared. The water flow and water pressure are quite comfortable! It can completely replace the regret I just said.

Catering and others:
The swimming pool is relatively average. There are no lockers, changing rooms, or even hair dryers, but the water temperature is quite comfortable.

The dinner at Sanwutang restaurant is delicious Beijing cuisine, which is very suitable for people with heavy tastes. The fried liver and stewed belly are very happy. But the Japanese food area there is really a disaster. The raw food and sushi are all unpalatable, even worse than the 60 yuan self-service sushi I went to before...

Overall, I am very satisfied. After all, I really enjoyed the rest. Five-star praise. Thanks again for the care of Manager Liang.

After the epidemic, with children staycation will go around to Xinguomao for a night or two
This year's Spring Festival is also
To be honest, compared with the magnificent and peninsula suites that I have lived in in the past two months, Xinguomao is indeed more suitable for families with children.
This only refers to the suites of Xinguomao, because once the suites were not sorted out, when we temporarily went to a single room to rest, in addition to the size of the ordinary rooms, the room facilities were also poor.
The suite here is bright, especially the south-facing room type, which is really comfortable to live in in winter.
There are free extra beds for children aged three or four, and the beds are spacious and comfortable
Basic toiletries are also prepared for children
On the 30th night, there are gift boxes for the New Year, some small snacks, it is good to appease the children
The next day was my birthday, and I also gave a small piece of cake and balloons
Although this is different from the peninsula hotel's birthday decoration, it is a distance from me to Son Yejin.
But yes, it's good
After all, the price difference is there
Another advantage is that the daily room rate itself includes the same day's dinner and the next day's breakfast, which saves you the headache of what to eat for dinner.
The New Year's 30 dinner menu is very rich. At first glance, there are many chicken, duck, and fish, but the taste is really ordinary.
This is a conscience of the buffet world
But the taste of this restaurant, especially the meat main course, is really indescribable. This is the first time I have eaten roast duck so arrogantly.
, My colleagues said that the staple food dim sum is not bad, but I don't eat it, so I can't evaluate it. Who would eat a lot of staple food for the New Year?
Drinks in the meal are also free, which is very good, and the corners improve the restaurant's price/performance ratio
Breakfast is also a staple food, which may be a problem of restaurant positioning. But eggs are also completely enough to eat.
The hotel gym is also a very popular gym of this generation. Like the Kerry Hotel, it is aimed at guests outside the hotel. It is characterized by a large area, complete facilities, and a good view. At the same time, there is a problem of many people. However, so many such expensive equipment are placed here, and it is difficult to return to the original.
There is no problem at all to kill an iron and aerobic swim for two or three hours.
If I can't leave Beijing for a day, I will still come here. I don't know if I can get familiar with it.
